# Shared Memory Bridge
Atlas (Hermes) <-> subbots / voice app. Subbots READ "ATLAS CONTEXT"; everyone APPENDS to "SUBBOT LOG".
Atlas distills SUBBOT LOG into MEMORY.md periodically. This is the single source of truth
so every spun-up subbot and the voice app operate from the same facts as Atlas.

## ATLAS CONTEXT
- Identity: Atlas is Tom Torok's AI co-worker (Hermes Agent). The voice app uses the SAME Atlas brain (hy3) — it IS Atlas, not a sub-bot.
- User: Tom Torok, Falls Church VA. Co-owns Paw Prints pet care (Falls Church) with wife Jane. Son Carson.
- Comms: Telegram primary. Prefers concise markdown, autonomy, diagnosis-before-action, timelines with time estimates.
- Network: Tailscale — Charles 100.115.214.128 (charles-1.taila0a481.ts.net). Phone oneplus-10t-5g.
- Atlas Voice Butler (Charles): Parakeet STT (local) + hy3 brain (direct OpenRouter) + chatterbox TTS (local Atlas voice). ~10s round trip.
- Paw Prints: local pet care, brand colors Sunny Yellow #FFF386 / Gold #FFD000 / Grass Green #5CBF2A / Dark Brown #3D2E25 / Cream #FFF8E1. Jane = face/ops, Tom = strategy/tech.
- Coaching: AI Profit Boardroom (Skool skool.com/ai-profit-lab-7462). Thu 11AM coaching + Mon/Wed/Fri coffee hours.
- Free-model stance: stay free; reject paid (deepseek-v4-pro, $20 ChatGPT). hy3:free current brain; nemotron-nano fallback.
- Memory convention: append notable voice-app exchanges to SUBBOT LOG so Atlas can fold them into long-term memory.
- KEY FACTS (2026-07-14): UA1445 (United) departs IAD 9:12 PM EDT, gate D12, on time. Drive Falls Church->IAD ~31 min. Tom opted to keep voice-app brain = hy3 (Atlas, not a sub-bot); shared-memory bridge built so all spun-up subbots read this context. Tom: beef enchilada recipe
Atlas: Here's a quick beef enchilada recipe:

Brown 1 lb ground beef with diced onion, then stir in 1 can enchilada sauce (reserve 1/2 cup), cumin, chili powder, and 1 cup shredded cheese. Soften corn tortillas in hot oil, fill with the beef mix, roll up, and place seam-down in a baking dish. Top with remaining sauce and cheese, bake at 350°F for 20 minutes. Serve with sour cream and cilantro.
